RegExp(stringFound[1],"g"),newSlot);}}adsNinjaWinnerAds[x][i]=w;}}}else{var f=adsNinja_battle(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(adsByZone[x])));if(f!=null){if(f.isDfp==1){var newSlot=stringFound[1]+"_"+String(f.idPageTemplateZone)+"_"+String(1);newSlot=newSlot.replace(/-/g,"_");f.content=f.content.replace(new RegExp(stringFound[1],"g"),newSlot);}}adsNinjaWinnerAds[x]=f;}}}if(typeof safeTraffic!=='undefined'&&!safeTraffic){adsNinjaWinnerAds=[];}for(x in adsNinjaWinnerAds){if(adsNinjaWinnerAds[x].constructor===Array){for(y in adsNinjaWinnerAds[x]){var winnerAd=adsNinjaWinnerAds[x][y];if(winnerAd.isDfp==1){var fn=window[functionName];if(typeof fn==="function"){fn();console.log("Ads Ninja 2.0 : called fn : "+functionName);}}}}}else{var winnerAd=adsNinjaWinnerAds[x];if(winnerAd.isDfp==1){var functionNamefound=winnerAd.content.match(/googletag\.display\('([a-z0-9_-]+)'\);/i);if(functionNamefound){var functionName=functionNamefound[1];functionName="f"+functionName.replace(/-/g,"_");var fn=window[functionName];if(typeof fn==="function"){fn();console.log("Ads Ninja 2.0 : called fn : "+functionName);}}}}}console.log("Ads Ninja 2.0 winners : ");console.log(adsNinjaWinnerAds);</script>
